a) What is the acceleration of the particle?
b) What additional force must act on the particle to give it an acceleration of 2i ^GaCk5FLR

30i + 25j + 50i - 30j - 10gj = 10a ^4Z6gnqaY

80i  - 5j - 10gj = 10a

a = 8i - 10.3j
b) 80i - 10.3j = F = 10+2i
F = -60i + 103j ^yrbSW2av

Two forces of 5i + 2j and i - 3j act on a particle of mass 2kg which is initially moving at a velocity of u.
a) What is the acceleration of the particle?
b) The particle comes to rest after 4 seconds. Find u. ^jjiFhWum

F = ma
5i + 2j + i - 3j = 2a
a = 3i - 0.5j ^ddLj9a4R

b)

u = u
v = 0

t = 4 ^lmZgbmtq

v = u + at
0 = u + 4(3i - 0.5j)
0 = u + 12i - 2j
u = -12i + 2j ^Bz7z1gy7
